\DoxyCodeLine{607 \textcolor{comment}{// Helper: ImChunkStream<>}}
\DoxyCodeLine{608 \textcolor{comment}{// Build and iterate a contiguous stream of variable-\/sized structures.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{609 \textcolor{comment}{// This is used by Settings to store persistent data while reducing allocation count.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{610 \textcolor{comment}{// We store the chunk size first, and align the final size on 4 bytes boundaries.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{611 \textcolor{comment}{// The tedious/zealous amount of casting is to avoid -\/Wcast-\/align warnings.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{612 \textcolor{keyword}{template}<\textcolor{keyword}{typename} T>}
\DoxyCodeLine{613 \textcolor{keyword}{struct }IMGUI\_API \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_im_chunk_stream}{ImChunkStream}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{614 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{615     \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_im_vector}{ImVector<char>}}  Buf;}
\DoxyCodeLine{616 }
\DoxyCodeLine{617     \textcolor{keywordtype}{void}    clear()                     \{ Buf.clear(); \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{618     \textcolor{keywordtype}{bool}    empty()\textcolor{keyword}{ const               }\{ \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} Buf.Size == 0; \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{619     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int}     size()\textcolor{keyword}{ const                }\{ \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} Buf.Size; \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{620     T*      alloc\_chunk(\textcolor{keywordtype}{size\_t} sz)      \{ \textcolor{keywordtype}{size\_t} HDR\_SZ = 4; sz = IM\_MEMALIGN(HDR\_SZ + sz, 4u); \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} off = Buf.Size; Buf.resize(off + (\textcolor{keywordtype}{int})sz); ((\textcolor{keywordtype}{int}*)(\textcolor{keywordtype}{void}*)(Buf.Data + off))[0] = (int)sz; \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} (T*)(\textcolor{keywordtype}{void}*)(Buf.Data + off + (\textcolor{keywordtype}{int})HDR\_SZ); \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{621     T*      begin()                     \{ \textcolor{keywordtype}{size\_t} HDR\_SZ = 4; \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (!Buf.Data) \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} NULL; \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} (T*)(\textcolor{keywordtype}{void}*)(Buf.Data + HDR\_SZ); \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{622     T*      next\_chunk(T* p)            \{ \textcolor{keywordtype}{size\_t} HDR\_SZ = 4; IM\_ASSERT(p >= begin() \&\& p < end()); p = (T*)(\textcolor{keywordtype}{void}*)((\textcolor{keywordtype}{char}*)(\textcolor{keywordtype}{void}*)p + chunk\_size(p)); \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (p == (T*)(\textcolor{keywordtype}{void}*)((\textcolor{keywordtype}{char}*)end() + HDR\_SZ)) \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} (T*)0; IM\_ASSERT(p < end()); \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} p; \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{623     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int}     chunk\_size(\textcolor{keyword}{const} T* p)      \{ \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} ((\textcolor{keyword}{const} \textcolor{keywordtype}{int}*)p)[-\/1]; \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{624     T*      end()                       \{ \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} (T*)(\textcolor{keywordtype}{void}*)(Buf.Data + Buf.Size); \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{625     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int}     offset\_from\_ptr(\textcolor{keyword}{const} T* p) \{ IM\_ASSERT(p >= begin() \&\& p < end()); \textcolor{keyword}{const} ptrdiff\_t off = (\textcolor{keyword}{const} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char}*)p -\/ Buf.Data; return (\textcolor{keywordtype}{int})off; \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{626     T*      ptr\_from\_offset(\textcolor{keywordtype}{int} off)    \{ IM\_ASSERT(off >= 4 \&\& off < Buf.Size); \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} (T*)(\textcolor{keywordtype}{void}*)(Buf.Data + off); \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{627     \textcolor{keywordtype}{void}    swap(\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_im_chunk_stream}{ImChunkStream<T>}}\& rhs) \{ rhs.Buf.swap(Buf); \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{628 }
\DoxyCodeLine{629 \};}
\DoxyCodeLine{630 }
\DoxyCodeLine{631 \textcolor{comment}{//-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{632 \textcolor{comment}{// [SECTION] ImDrawList support}}
\DoxyCodeLine{633 \textcolor{comment}{//-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{634 }
\DoxyCodeLine{635 \textcolor{comment}{// ImDrawList: Helper function to calculate a circle's segment count given its radius and a "{}maximum error"{} value.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{636 \textcolor{comment}{// Estimation of number of circle segment based on error is derived using method described in https://stackoverflow.com/a/2244088/15194693}}
\DoxyCodeLine{637 \textcolor{comment}{// Number of segments (N) is calculated using equation:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{638 \textcolor{comment}{//   N = ceil ( pi / acos(1 -\/ error / r) )     where r > 0, error <= r}}
\DoxyCodeLine{639 \textcolor{comment}{// Our equation is significantly simpler that one in the post thanks for choosing segment that is}}
\DoxyCodeLine{640 \textcolor{comment}{// perpendicular to X axis. Follow steps in the article from this starting condition and you will}}
\DoxyCodeLine{641 \textcolor{comment}{// will get this result.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{642 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{643 \textcolor{comment}{// Rendering circles with an odd number of segments, while mathematically correct will produce}}
\DoxyCodeLine{644 \textcolor{comment}{// asymmetrical results on the raster grid. Therefore we're rounding N to next even number (7-\/>8, 8-\/>8, 9-\/>10 etc.)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{645 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{646 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define IM\_ROUNDUP\_TO\_EVEN(\_V)                                  ((((\_V) + 1) / 2) * 2)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{647 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define IM\_DRAWLIST\_CIRCLE\_AUTO\_SEGMENT\_MIN                     4}}
\DoxyCodeLine{648 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define IM\_DRAWLIST\_CIRCLE\_AUTO\_SEGMENT\_MAX                     512}}
\DoxyCodeLine{649 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define IM\_DRAWLIST\_CIRCLE\_AUTO\_SEGMENT\_CALC(\_RAD,\_MAXERROR)    ImClamp(IM\_ROUNDUP\_TO\_EVEN((int)ImCeil(IM\_PI / ImAcos(1 -\/ ImMin((\_MAXERROR), (\_RAD)) / (\_RAD)))), IM\_DRAWLIST\_CIRCLE\_AUTO\_SEGMENT\_MIN, IM\_DRAWLIST\_CIRCLE\_AUTO\_SEGMENT\_MAX)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{650 }
\DoxyCodeLine{651 \textcolor{comment}{// Raw equation from IM\_DRAWLIST\_CIRCLE\_AUTO\_SEGMENT\_CALC rewritten for 'r' and 'error'.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{652 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define IM\_DRAWLIST\_CIRCLE\_AUTO\_SEGMENT\_CALC\_R(\_N,\_MAXERROR)    ((\_MAXERROR) / (1 -\/ ImCos(IM\_PI / ImMax((float)(\_N), IM\_PI))))}}
\DoxyCodeLine{653 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define IM\_DRAWLIST\_CIRCLE\_AUTO\_SEGMENT\_CALC\_ERROR(\_N,\_RAD)     ((1 -\/ ImCos(IM\_PI / ImMax((float)(\_N), IM\_PI))) / (\_RAD))}}
\DoxyCodeLine{654 }
\DoxyCodeLine{655 \textcolor{comment}{// ImDrawList: Lookup table size for adaptive arc drawing, cover full circle.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{656 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#ifndef IM\_DRAWLIST\_ARCFAST\_TABLE\_SIZE}}
\DoxyCodeLine{657 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define IM\_DRAWLIST\_ARCFAST\_TABLE\_SIZE                          48 }\textcolor{comment}{// Number of samples in lookup table.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{658 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#endif}}
\DoxyCodeLine{659 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define IM\_DRAWLIST\_ARCFAST\_SAMPLE\_MAX                          IM\_DRAWLIST\_ARCFAST\_TABLE\_SIZE }\textcolor{comment}{// Sample index \_PathArcToFastEx() for 360 angle.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{660 }

\DoxyCodeLine{2592     \textcolor{comment}{// Docking -\/ Builder function needs to be generally called before the node is used/submitted.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2593     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ The DockBuilderXXX functions are designed to \_eventually\_ become a public API, but it is too early to expose it and guarantee stability.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2594     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Do not hold on ImGuiDockNode* pointers! They may be invalidated by any split/merge/remove operation and every frame.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2595     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ To create a DockSpace() node, make sure to set the ImGuiDockNodeFlags\_DockSpace flag when calling DockBuilderAddNode().}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2596     \textcolor{comment}{//   You can create dockspace nodes (attached to a window) \_or\_ floating nodes (carry its own window) with this API.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2597     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ DockBuilderSplitNode() create 2 child nodes within 1 node. The initial node becomes a parent node.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2598     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ If you intend to split the node immediately after creation using DockBuilderSplitNode(), make sure}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2599     \textcolor{comment}{//   to call DockBuilderSetNodeSize() beforehand. If you don't, the resulting split sizes may not be reliable.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2600     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/ Call DockBuilderFinish() after you are done.}}
